[30;1m733 | [0m[35m## Manipulating DataFrame Models post-definition[0m
[30;1m734 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m735 | [0m[35mOne caveat of using inheritance to build schemas on top of each other is that there[0m
[30;1m736 | [0m[35mis no clear way of how a child class can e.g. remove fields or update them without[0m
[30;1m737 | [0m[35mcompletely overriding previous settings. This is because inheritance is strictly additive.[0m
[30;1m738 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m739 | [0m[35m{class}`~pandera.api.pandas.container.DataFrameSchema` objects do have these options though, as desc[0m
